23 /**
24  * Helper class to get the consumer friendly device name.</p>
25  *
26  * {@code String device = Devices.getDeviceName();}</p>
27  *
28  * The above code will get the device name as specified in the supported device list that is
29  * maintained by Google.</p>
30  *
31  * See: https://support.google.com/googleplay/answer/1727131</p>
32  *
33  * @author Jared Rummler <jared.rummler@gmail.com>
34  */
35 public class Devices {
36

3577  private static String sDeviceName;
3578 
3579  /** Returns the consumer friendly device name */
3580  public static String getDeviceName() {
3581  if (sDeviceName != null) {
3582  return sDeviceName;
3583  }
3584  final String key = Build.DEVICE + "|" + Build.MODEL;
3585  for (final String str : SUPPORTED_DEVICES) {
3586  if (str.endsWith(key)) {
3587  final String[] names = str.split("\\|");
3588  final String retailBranding = names[0];
3589  final String marketingName = names[1];
3590  if (marketingName.startsWith(retailBranding)) {
3591  sDeviceName = marketingName;
3592  } else {
3593  sDeviceName = retailBranding + " " + marketingName;
3594  }
3595  return sDeviceName;
3596  }
3597  }
3598  final String manufacturer = Build.MANUFACTURER;
3599  final String model = Build.MODEL;
3600  if (model.startsWith(manufacturer)) {
3601  sDeviceName = capitalize(model);
3602  } else if (manufacturer.equalsIgnoreCase("HTC")) {
3603  sDeviceName = "HTC " + model; // make sure HTC is capitalized
3604  } else {
3605  sDeviceName = capitalize(manufacturer) + " " + model;
3606  }
3607  return sDeviceName;
3608  }
3609 
3610  /** Returns the consumer friendly device name based on the value of {@link Build#DEVICE} */
3611  public static String getDeviceName(final String device) {
3612  final String key = "|" + device + "|";
3613  for (final String str : SUPPORTED_DEVICES) {
3614  if (str.contains(key)) {
3615  final String[] names = str.split("\\|");
3616  final String retailBranding = names[0];
3617  final String marketingName = names[1];
3618  if (marketingName.startsWith(retailBranding)
3619  || marketingName.toLowerCase(Locale.ENGLISH).startsWith("moto ")) {
3620  return marketingName;
3621  }
3622  return retailBranding + " " + marketingName;
3623  }
3624  }
3625  return null;
3626  }
3627 
3628  /**
3629  * <p>
3630  * Capitalizes all the whitespace separated words in a String. Only the first letter of each
3631  * word is changed. To convert the rest of each word to lowercase at the same time, use
3632  * {@link #capitalizeFully(String)}.
3633  * </p>
3634  *
3635  * <p>
3636  * Whitespace is defined by {@link Character#isWhitespace(char)}.
3637  * </p>
3638  *
3639  * @param str
3640  * the String to capitalize
3641  * @return capitalized The capitalized String
3642  */
3643  private static final String capitalize(final String str) {
3644  if (TextUtils.isEmpty(str)) {
3645  return str;
3646  }
3647  final char[] arr = str.toCharArray();
3648  boolean capitalizeNext = true;
3649  String phrase = "";
3650  for (final char c : arr) {
3651  if (capitalizeNext && Character.isLetter(c)) {
3652  phrase += Character.toUpperCase(c);
3653  capitalizeNext = false;
3654  continue;
3655  } else if (Character.isWhitespace(c)) {
3656  capitalizeNext = true;
3657  }
3658  phrase += c;
3659  }
3660  return phrase;
3661  }
